# Beat the House ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ 0.3.2 Low-End & Web Cleanup Board

Created: 2026-07-04
Owner: project management
Scope: 0.3.2 is the main cleanup pass of the v0.3 set. NO new content, NO new
features. The mission is exhaustive: identify and review EVERY function in the
production codebase for lag, per-frame cost, memory that is allocated and never
released, allocation churn, and anything else that makes the game run slowly on
a low-end system or in the web export ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ then fix what is found.

How this board differs from 0.3.1: the 0.3.1 Performance & Stability Audit was
symptom-driven (chase the known hot spots, fence them with budgets). This board
is coverage-driven: a function-level census of the whole repository where every
production function gets classified, every hot-class function gets read and
costed, and the low-end/web target ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ never measured in 0.3.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ becomes the
budget baseline. Nothing is exempt because "it was fine on the dev box".

Known leads this board exists to run down (verify and extend, do not
rediscover):

- Every 0.3.1 performance number was measured headless or on a 4070 Ti
  desktop. The web export (`builds/itch/BeatTheHouse-web.zip`, 16.3 MB) and
  low-end hardware have NEVER been profiled. Web is single-threaded WASM with
  slower allocation, slower JSON, and a stricter memory ceiling; the SC.2
  budget table has no web or min-spec column.
- SC.3's final soak recorded a POSITIVE memory slope of 719,852 bytes/sample
  (~4.3 MB/simulated hour) where SA.4's soak had measured -455,080 bytes
  post-warmup. The cap assert passed; the slope reversal was never explained.
- The pinball feature's structural cost is documented and unfixed:
  docs/plans/pinball_feature_rework_plan.md ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓЖ’Гўв‚¬ЕЎГѓвЂљГ‚В§1 records per-tick
  read_machine -> duplicate(true) -> write_machine round-tripping of the whole
  machine dict including the live session, O(history) copy growth, Variant
  dictionary math, and per-step TableScript.new(). 0.3.1's SB.1 explicitly
  made "no edits inside pinball internals"; `pinball_feature.gd` still
  contains 7 `duplicate(` calls today.
- docs/plans/dead_code_audit_report.md (2026-07-01) is a READ-ONLY audit with
  a prescribed removal sequence that was only partially executed (R9 removed
  speculative_content.md). Dead scripts, dead data keys, and unreferenced
  assets still ship in the export.
- The audio stack ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ `procedural_music_player.gd` (3,542 lines),
  `sfx_player.gd` (1,904 lines), `web_audio_bridge.gd` ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ was reworked for web
  playback late in 0.3.1 (commit `6ae682b`) and has never had a performance
  or allocation audit. Procedural music synthesizes/schedules continuously,
  which is exactly the kind of steady per-frame cost a low-end machine feels.
- Roulette's enforced resolve budget is 16/18/20 ms avg/p95/max on the dev
  box ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ already more than a whole frame at 60 FPS. On a low-end machine or
  web that is a multi-frame hitch on every spin.
- Size concentration: `foundation_main.gd` 11,154 lines, `blackjack.gd`
  5,684, `run_state.gd` 4,083, `pixel_scene_canvas.gd` 3,843. The census must
  not skip the big files because they are big.

---

## Low-end target definition

All budgets on this board are set against two targets, not the dev box:

- **MIN-SPEC DESKTOP**: 2015-class dual-core laptop CPU with integrated
  graphics. Approximated on the dev box by the measured low-end scale factor
  from L0.2: **10.2x** for scaled per-frame headroom checks until a physical
  min-spec machine replaces the browser-throttle proxy.
- **WEB**: the itch.io HTML5 export running in current Chrome and Firefox on
  the same class of hardware. Measured directly via the L0.2 web harness, not
  approximated.

A change "passes" only if the dev-box numbers leave headroom for the scale
factor, or the web harness measures it directly under budget.

---

## Shared task guideline

Prepend this block to every task prompt below (referred to as
`[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]`).

```text
You are a senior Godot 4 / GDScript engineer working the 0.3.2 Low-End & Web
Cleanup board for Beat the House.

WORKSPACE: D:\Projects\Beat-The-House
ENGINE: Godot 4.6-compatible, Windows/PowerShell. Run via tools/run_godot.ps1.
Web builds via tools/export_itch.ps1 -Target web, served by tools/serve_web.ps1.

MISSION: 0.3.2 is the main cleanup pass of the v0.3 set. Do not add content
or features. Review every function in your task's scope for per-frame cost,
per-action cost, allocation churn, retained memory, and low-end/web impact.
Read the relevant files before editing. Measure before and after every
performance change; a perf fix without numbers is not done. Do not stop at
analysis unless the task explicitly says it is documentation-only.

SOURCES OF TRUTH:
- README.md (top-level spec).
- docs/plans/0.3.2_low_end_web_cleanup_board.md (this board).
- docs/plans/0.3.1_perf_stability_audit_board.md (prior hardening pass; its
  SC.2 budget table governs existing budgets ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ read it BEFORE changing any
  draw, resolve, suite-time, or static-scan budget, and record fresh
  measurements here when re-baselining).
- docs/plans/0.3.2_function_census.md (produced by L0.1; every sweep task
  consumes it).
- docs/plans/pinball_feature_rework_plan.md (LA.4 context).
- docs/plans/dead_code_audit_report.md (LC.1 context).

ARCHITECTURE CONTRACTS:
- RunState is authoritative; game modules return result dictionaries applied
  via GameModule.apply_result or RunActionService. Never mutate
  bankroll/heat/inventory directly from a surface.
- Deterministic RNG only: RngStream forks. Never randomize()/randf()/randi().
  The two-process determinism probe (foundation_determinism_probe.ps1) must
  stay green after any change to state or resolve paths.
- Content is data-driven JSON under data/ loaded via ContentLibrary.
- Save/load must round-trip any state you touch; the SB.3 interrupt-fuzz
  fixture and 0.3.0 compatibility fixture must stay green.
- Per-frame code paths must be zero-copy: no duplicate(true), no JSON
  stringify, no full-table reads inside _process/_draw or per-frame checks.
  The SA.2 tripwire enforces this; waivers need SA2_PER_FRAME_OK reasons.
- Peeked dictionaries are read-only; the SB.2 mutation firewall must stay
  green.

GDSCRIPT STRICTNESS: warnings are errors; type locals from dictionaries; use
clampi/clampf/mini/maxf etc.

LOW-END RULE: budgets are judged against the min-spec scale factor and the
web harness from L0.2, not the dev box alone. A fix that only helps a 4070 Ti
is not a fix.

VALIDATION LOOP: measure -> fix root cause -> add a regression test or budget
assert so it cannot come back -> run the narrowest suite -> run the task DONE
gate -> record before/after numbers in the board.

FIX DISCIPLINE:
- Root causes only. No timeout raises, no assertion weakening, no skipped
  tests, no "accepted baseline" without this board recording evidence.
- Every perf fix records before/after numbers (ms, MB, bytes/frame, or suite
  seconds) with the measurement command.
- Every bug fix adds a permanent foundation_check fixture reproducing it.
- Sweep tasks record a per-function disposition table: every hot-class
  function in scope gets a row (OK / fixed / waived-with-reason). "I looked
  at the file" is not evidence; the table is.
- Each completed task commits its own work; evidence lines include the
  commit hash.

DEFAULT GATE:
powershell -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File tools/validate_project.ps1
powershell -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File tools/check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot

DONE STATUS RULE: a task may not be marked DONE while any command in its DONE
gate fails or crashes. Partial passes must set status VERIFY with the failing
command named and a clear next step.

End with evidence: commands run, pass/fail output, before/after numbers,
file:line summary, disposition table where required. Update this task's
status line in the board when done.
```

Priorities: **P0** blocks 0.3.2. **P1** required cleanup. **P2** cut
candidate. Statuses: BACKLOG / IN PROGRESS / VERIFY / DONE (with evidence).

Recommended execution order: L0.1 and L0.2 first (census and low-end truth ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ
everything else consumes them), then LB.1 (memory slope) and LA.4 (pinball) as
the two biggest known structural items, then the LA sweeps in any order, then
LB.2/LB.3, then LC, then LD last.

---

## Epic 0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Census & Low-End Truth

**L0.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Function-Level Cost Census of the Entire Production Codebase** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: none ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: DONE

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK L0.1 - Build the complete function inventory this board audits against.
Documentation and tooling only; zero behavior fixes in this task.

Every later sweep task claims "every function in scope was reviewed". That
claim is only checkable against a generated census, not vibes.

1. Build tools/function_census.gd (headless) or a PowerShell equivalent that
   parses every production .gd file (scripts/core, scripts/games, scripts/ui;
   tests and tools listed but flagged non-shipping) and emits, per function:
   file, name, line span, line count, static/instance, and every call
   signal it can classify mechanically: reachable from _process /
   _physics_process / _draw / _input / *_per_frame / *_needs_auto_tick /
   *_runtime_needs_tick (PER-FRAME class), from resolve/apply_result/
   surface action dispatch (PER-ACTION class), from _ready/ContentLibrary
   load (STARTUP class), from to_dict/from_dict/normalize (SAVE-LOAD class),
   else UNCLASSIFIED. A function may hold multiple classes; classification
   is by call-graph reachability (one-level textual call tracing is
   acceptable; record the method's limitations honestly).
2. Emit docs/plans/0.3.2_function_census.json (machine) and
   docs/plans/0.3.2_function_census.md (human summary: counts per class per
   file, the full PER-FRAME list, the full PER-ACTION list, and the
   UNCLASSIFIED list ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ UNCLASSIFIED functions are census debt the sweeps
   must manually classify, not skip).
3. Assign every production file to exactly one owning sweep task (LA.1,
   LA.2, LA.3, LA.4, LA.5, LA.6) in a coverage table in this board. No file
   may be unowned; foundation_check.gd and ui_scene_compile_check.gd are
   owned by whichever sweep touches their fixtures but are exempt from
   shipping-cost review (they never ship).
4. Wire the census generator into validate_project.ps1 as a freshness check
   (regenerate and diff; a stale census fails validation) so the census
   cannot rot after this board closes.

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1 (with freshness check active);
check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot; census .json and .md committed; coverage
table in this board maps every production file to an owning task.
```

Evidence 2026-07-04: `tools/function_census.ps1` generated
`docs/plans/0.3.2_function_census.json` and
`docs/plans/0.3.2_function_census.md`; census covers 75 files, 51 shipping
files, 5,244 total functions, 3,872 shipping functions, 1,221 PER-FRAME
functions, 1,917 PER-ACTION functions, 627 STARTUP functions, 860 SAVE-LOAD
functions, and 2,273 UNCLASSIFIED functions. `tools/validate_project.ps1`
wires a deterministic regenerate-and-diff freshness check. Coverage table
maps all 51 shipping files exactly once. Gates: `tools/function_census.ps1
-Check` PASS; `tools/validate_project.ps1` PASS; `tools/check_godot.ps1
-RequireGodot` PASS (Smoke summary: validate_project 13,610ms, godot_import
10,700ms, gdscript_load_check 9,175ms, foundation_smoke 24,062ms,
ui_scene_compile 48,825ms, roulette_audio_audit 2,630ms,
foundation_perf_smoke 8,383ms). Commit: `a555bba`.

**L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Web & Min-Spec Baseline Harness** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: none ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: DONE

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK L0.2 - Measure the game where it is actually slow: the web export and a
min-spec approximation. Produce the baseline table every budget on this
board is judged against.

0.3.1 shipped budgets measured on a 4070 Ti. This task creates the missing
low-end truth.

1. In-game perf telemetry: add a debug-only perf overlay/telemetry hook
   (enabled by URL query or OS.get_cmdline flag, stripped from release UX)
   that samples frame time, process time, physics time, draw calls
   (Performance.RENDER_*), static memory, and object/node counts, and can
   dump a JSON report ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ in the running game, including the web build, via
   JavaScriptBridge console output on web. Keep the overlay itself under
   0.1ms/frame (it must not be its own heisenbug).
2. Web baseline: export web (export_itch.ps1 -Target web), serve
   (serve_web.ps1), and measure in Chrome and Firefox: page-load-to-menu
   time (cold cache and warm), per-surface idle and active frame times for
   all seven games, slot autoplay, a pinball feature session, world map,
   and 10 minutes of scripted play memory growth. Record browser, CPU
   throttle setting, and numbers. Use Chrome DevTools CPU throttling (4x
   and 6x) as the min-spec proxy in-browser.
3. Min-spec desktop factor: on the dev box, measure the same scripted
   scenarios in the desktop build, then derive and document the measured
   web/dev-box and throttled/unthrottled cost ratios. Publish the chosen
   LOW-END SCALE FACTOR (with derivation) in this board; the LD.1 budgets
   use it.
4. Baseline appendix in this board: every scenario -> desktop ms / web ms /
   throttled web ms / memory. Flag every scenario whose throttled-web frame
   time exceeds 16.6ms ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ that flagged list is the priority input for the
   LA sweeps.
5. Zero fixes in this task beyond the telemetry hook itself.

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot; telemetry
hook merged with its own cost measured; baseline appendix committed with
desktop, web, and throttled-web numbers for every listed scenario; scale
factor published.
```

Evidence 2026-07-04: added `scripts/ui/perf_telemetry_overlay.gd` and the
`tools/l02_desktop_perf_probe.ps1` / `tools/l02_web_perf_probe.mjs` drivers.
Telemetry is dormant unless enabled with `--bth-perf-telemetry`,
`--bth-perf-plan=l02`, or `?bth_perf=1&bth_perf_plan=l02`; web reports are
captured through `JavaScriptBridge` console lines. Final web export:
`tools/export_itch.ps1 -Target web` PASS, SHA256
`C14BC2F0235EC88C8A0329BE64492AE8C16A2B5E68FB5A8EB552CEA5E4E2DB28`.

Telemetry hook cost, final stride-30 build: desktop dry avg 0.001351ms/frame,
p95 0.002ms; Chrome cold dry avg 0.003695ms, p95 0.010ms; Chrome warm dry
avg 0.003787ms, p95 0.010ms; Chrome 4x dry avg 0.029435ms (amortized),
sample-frame p95 0.170ms; Chrome 6x full avg 0.065222ms (amortized),
sample-frame p95 0.190ms; Firefox cold full avg 0.009463ms, p95 0.021ms.
The 4x and 6x p95 values are monitor-sample frames; amortized per-frame hook
cost stays below the 0.1ms target. Firefox does not expose `performance.memory`
through this harness, so Firefox memory deltas are recorded as unavailable
(`0`) and Chrome heap deltas are the web memory source.

Browser/load baseline: Chrome 149.0.7827.115 / user agent
`Chrome/149.0.0.0`, Firefox 151.0 / user agent `Firefox/151.0`. Chrome final
cold load-to-ready 3,068ms; Chrome final warm load-to-ready 2,478ms; Chrome
4x cold load-to-ready 13,996ms; Chrome 6x cold load-to-ready 26,993ms.
Firefox cold load-to-ready 10,405ms; Firefox warm load-to-ready 8,378ms.

LOW-END SCALE FACTOR: **10.2x**. Derivation: max Chrome warm web / desktop
p95 ratio was 1.276x (`baccarat_active`); max Chrome 6x / Chrome warm p95
ratio was 10.144x (`world_map_idle`); max Chrome 6x / desktop p95 ratio was
9.604x (`blackjack_active`). LD.1 should use 10.2x for scaled per-frame
budget checks until a physical min-spec machine replaces this proxy. Chrome
4x full scenario frame-time numbers were captured before the stride-30
telemetry reduction; they are retained as conservative frame-time baselines
because the old hook sampled expensive monitors more often, while the final
hook cost is measured above.

| pull_tabs_idle | 15.309 | 8.333 | 18.608 | 44.361 | 50.984 | 17.171 | 2.687 | 0.521 | YES |
| pull_tabs_active | 15.671 | 8.071 | 30.418 | 42.004 | 52.307 | 1.133 | -1.237 | -0.211 | YES |

## Epic A ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Full-Function Sweeps

Every sweep task: consume the L0.1 census for your files; manually classify
your UNCLASSIFIED functions; read every PER-FRAME and PER-ACTION class
function in scope; profile suspects with Time.get_ticks_usec deltas (10k-rep
micro-harness or probe scenario); fix confirmed costs; record the
per-function disposition table. Prioritize anything L0.2 flagged red.

**LA.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Core State & Services Sweep** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.1, L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: DONE

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LA.1 - Function-level audit of scripts/core: run_state.gd,
run_action_service.gd, game_module.gd, run_generator.gd, world_map.gd,

Specific suspicions to confirm or clear (extend, don't limit to):
1. run_state.gd (4,083 lines): to_dict/from_dict cost and allocation volume
   ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ autosave frequency times serialization cost is a recurring hitch
   source; normalization passes that deep-copy defensively where the input
   is already owned; history/log structures (verify the SA.4 caps actually
   bound allocation, not just length).
2. run_action_service.gd: per-presentation-view list rebuilds ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ are
   view/option lists rebuilt per open, per frame, or per click, and how
   much of each rebuild is recomputing static content data?
3. content_library.gd: JSON parse volume at startup, repeated lookups that
   re-walk arrays instead of indexed dictionaries, any lookup called from a
   PER-FRAME census class.
4. world_map.gd + run_generator.gd: generation is one-shot but travel-time
   snapshot/refresh paths run per travel ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ measure a travel transition on
   throttled web (L0.2 scenario) and attribute its cost.
5. save_service.gd: synchronous disk writes on the main thread ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ measure
   autosave stall on web (IndexedDB-backed user:// is slow); if the stall
   exceeds a frame, buffer/defer without weakening the SB.3 guarantees.
6. rng_stream.gd + card_shoe.gd: these are inner-loop primitives; verify
   fork/draw are allocation-light since every game pays them per resolve.

Per the sweep rules: disposition table for every PER-FRAME and PER-ACTION
function in these files; before/after numbers for every fix; determinism
probe and save fuzz must stay green (this task touches both risk areas).

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot
-FoundationSuite systems and contracts; foundation_determinism_probe.ps1
-SeedCount 10 -RequireGodot; foundation_performance_probe.ps1 -RequireGodot;

```

Evidence 2026-07-04: LA.1 audited 295 current PER-FRAME/PER-ACTION census rows across the owned core scope. Confirmed no PER-FRAME functions in the scoped core files; all hot rows are PER-ACTION. Fixes landed: world-map target/snapshot helpers now use prepared visible/node/edge lookups instead of repeated full graph copies; card-shoe draw/count/composition no longer clone the full shoe for read paths; normal web autosaves are queued/coalesced through the existing pending-autosave path while forced/manual saves remain synchronous; save files now write compact JSON and rely on close() instead of explicit flush(). Regression coverage: `card_shoe_core_primitives` in `foundation_check.gd`. Measurement harness: `tools/la1_core_perf_probe.gd`; web measurement used `bth_perf_plan=la1` through the L0.2 Chrome harness. Commit: 0a0627e085c0c0a9c9ad51af46e47f1c18424fe8.

**LA.3 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Slot Stack Sweep (Non-Pinball)** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.1, L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: DONE

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LA.3 - Function-level audit of slot.gd, slot_machine_state.gd,
slot_resolver.gd, slot_renderer.gd (2,600 lines), slot_presentation.gd,
slot_catalog.gd, slot_family_buffalo.gd, slot_rng_math.gd,
slot_machine_generator.gd. Pinball internals are LA.4's; do not double-fix.

Specific suspicions to confirm or clear (extend, don't limit to):
1. slot_renderer.gd during active spin: reel motion redraws every frame by
   design ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ audit what each frame redraws beyond the reels (cabinet chrome,
   paytable, meters) and layer-split or cache what is static. Slot autoplay
   active draw is ~3.5ms avg on the 4070 Ti; that is the single biggest
   sanctioned per-frame cost in the game and the first thing a low-end
   machine feels. Target measurable reduction with identical visuals.
2. slot_presentation.gd surface_state: session copy cost during features
   (the rework plan notes it copies the session per render frame ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ measure
   the buffalo path here, pinball in LA.4).
3. slot_resolver.gd: per-spin grid/payout allocation; win attribution
   walks; free-game retriggering paths.
4. slot_family_buffalo.gd: hold-and-spin per-respin state copies; ways
   evaluation allocation per spin.
5. slot_machine_generator.gd + slot_catalog.gd: generation-time cost when
   entering a casino with many machines (L0.2 travel scenario feeds this).

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot
-FoundationSuite slot and slot_acceptance; foundation_performance_probe.ps1
-RequireGodot with before/after slot autoplay draw numbers;
slot_machine_deep_audit stage passes; disposition table in the board.
```

LA.3 Evidence - 2026-07-04

Scope audited: `slot.gd`, `slot_machine_state.gd`, `slot_resolver.gd`, `slot_renderer.gd`, `slot_presentation.gd`, `slot_catalog.gd`, `slot_family_buffalo.gd`, `slot_rng_math.gd`, `slot_machine_generator.gd`. Current hot/manual rows reviewed: 267. Files with no current PER-FRAME/PER-ACTION census rows were inspected as state/startup/generation dependencies: `slot_machine_state.gd`, `slot_catalog.gd`, `slot_rng_math.gd`, `slot_machine_generator.gd`. Pinball internals were not modified; LA.4 owns that runtime path.

Fix summary: `slot_renderer.gd` now avoids the QA-only buffalo gold scan in internal draw signatures, carries shared result-strip and buffalo board payloads through the active draw, replaces read-only deep copies in buffalo draw helpers with read views, reuses static buffalo spin-symbol cycles, and caches symbol-label mapping. Outcomes were unchanged; no resolver logic changed.

**LA.4 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Pinball Runtime: Retire the Per-Tick Copy Architecture** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.1, L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LA.4 - Execute the runtime/state-boundary portion of
docs/plans/pinball_feature_rework_plan.md: eliminate the per-tick deep-copy
round-tripping structurally. This is a cleanup-scope subset ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ keep the
current boards, feel, items, and feature rules EXACTLY as they play today;
the feel redesign in that plan stays out of 0.3.2.

The documented structure (plan ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓЖ’Гўв‚¬ЕЎГѓвЂљГ‚В§1, verify it still holds, then fix):
1. Live session as a runtime object: hold the active pinball session in a
   dedicated runtime class (RefCounted) owned by the module for the
   duration of the feature. Per-tick advancement mutates the runtime
   session in place ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ NO read_machine duplicate(true), NO write_machine
   round-trip per tick. Serialize the session into machine-dict form ONLY
   at save boundaries and feature completion; the SB.3 mid-feature
   save/load fixture defines exactly what must round-trip.
2. Kill O(history) copy growth: trim trajectories/event logs BEFORE any
   copy is taken; history entries store bounded summaries, not full
   per-step trajectories.
3. Stop re-instantiating TableScript per step/query/sync; hold one.
4. Hot inner loop de-boxing where measured: ball position/velocity as
   Vector2 and packed arrays inside the runtime sim where it does not
   change serialized shape or outcomes.
5. Determinism is non-negotiable: identical inputs must produce identical
   feature outcomes and identical serialized state before vs after. Fence
   with the determinism probe's pinball checkpoints plus
   slot_pinball_physics_audit; if current probes don't hash mid-feature
   state, extend them first so the refactor is provably outcome-neutral.
6. Measure: per-tick cost and frame time during an active pinball feature,
   before/after, dev box AND throttled web (L0.2 scenario). This was the
   original "game-wide slowdown during the feature" complaint ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ the number
   that matters is the web one.

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot
-FoundationSuite slot and slot_acceptance; slot_pinball_physics_audit and
slot_machine_deep_audit pass; foundation_determinism_probe.ps1 -SeedCount 10
-RequireGodot; SB.3 save fuzz green (systems suite); before/after per-tick
and frame-time table (dev + throttled web) in the board;
foundation_stuck_state_sweep.ps1 -SeedCount 200 -RequireGodot.
```

## Epic B ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Memory & Load

**LB.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Root-Cause the Positive Soak Memory Slope** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P0 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: none ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LB.1 - Explain and eliminate the memory growth SC.3 recorded, then
tighten the soak assert so unexplained growth fails.

Context: SA.4's soak measured post-warmup memory growth of -455,080 bytes
(healthy). SC.3's final-tree soak recorded a slope of +719,852 bytes/sample
(~4.3 MB per simulated hour) plus object slope +4.456/sample, and PASSED,
because the assert only checks the serialized-size cap and coarse growth.
Something merged between SA.4 (commit 0832402) and SC.3 (commit 7deb874)
retains memory. Suspect window includes SB.4 UI hardening, SB.5 determinism
timestamps, SB.6 watchdogs, SC.2 perf smoke, and the web-audio work.

1. Reproduce: rerun the SC.3 soak configuration on the current tree and
   confirm the slope. Then bisect by capability, not by commit only:
   extend foundation_soak_probe.gd to break memory/object growth down by
   source ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ per-type object counts (Performance.OBJECT_COUNT plus
   instance counts for Node, RefCounted subclasses of interest), RunState
   serialized size, ContentLibrary caches, audio players/buffers, pinball
   session cache, signal connection counts on long-lived autoloads.
2. Fix every identified retainer: unreleased nodes, growing caches without
   eviction, closures/lambdas held by signals on autoloads, arrays that
   append per action without the SA.4 caps.
3. Tighten the assert: post-warmup slope must be within a small documented
   tolerance of zero (state the tolerance and why); object-count slope
   likewise. The cap assert stays as a backstop but can no longer be the
   only line.
4. Run the tightened soak on the web export too if feasible via the L0.2
   telemetry (shorter duration acceptable; document browser memory
   readings) ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ web is where a 4.3 MB/hour leak actually kills sessions.

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot;
foundation_soak_probe.ps1 -RequireGodot -SimMinutes 180 with the tightened
slope asserts green; root-cause writeup (what retained, since when, fix)
in the board.
```

**LB.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Allocation-Churn & GC-Pressure Audit** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.1, L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LB.2 - Leaks are LB.1; this task is churn ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ memory allocated and freed
every frame/action. Ref-counted churn costs CPU on every frame and is
disproportionately expensive in WASM.

1. Instrument: extend the L0.2 telemetry to sample allocation-rate proxies
   per scenario (Performance.OBJECT_COUNT deltas per frame, static memory
   deltas per frame between GC-neutral points). Build a small
   alloc-counting harness for targeted functions (call 10k times, read
   memory/object deltas).
2. Sweep the census PER-FRAME and PER-ACTION classes for churn patterns
   the SA.2 tripwire does NOT catch: Array/Dictionary literals rebuilt per
   call, String concatenation and format-string building in hot paths
   (draw labels, debug strings computed even when unused), PackedArray
   resizing in loops, Callable allocation in loops, per-frame Vector2
   array literals in draw code, and temporary dictionaries used as ad-hoc
   tuples.
3. Fix the measured worst offenders: hoist literals to constants, reuse
   scratch buffers where single-threaded per-frame use is provable,
   precompute label strings on state change (dirty-flag) instead of per
   draw.
4. Extend the SA.2 static tripwire where a pattern is mechanically
   detectable (e.g., string % formatting inside _draw-reachable functions
   without a SA2_PER_FRAME_OK waiver) ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ same waiver discipline.
5. Record: top-10 churn sites before/after (bytes or objects per frame,
   scenario), and the tripwire extension diff.

DONE GATE: validate_project.ps1 (tripwire extension active);
check_godot.ps1 -RequireGodot -Suite Full; foundation_performance_probe.ps1
-RequireGodot; before/after churn table in the board.
```

**LB.3 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Startup, Load-Time & Export-Size Audit** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LB.3 - The first minute is where low-end and web users quit. Measure
and reduce boot, load, and first-interaction latency, and the web payload.

1. Instrument boot: timestamp the boot sequence (engine start -> autoloads
   -> ContentLibrary parse -> main menu interactive -> first run start ->
   first surface interactive) via the L0.2 telemetry. Record desktop and
   web (cold + warm cache).
2. ContentLibrary: total JSON parse ms at startup; lazy-load or
   post-menu-defer content packs not needed for the main menu, if the

   suite.
3. First-open hitches: first time each game surface opens (font/theme
   compile, texture upload, shader compile). Godot compiles canvas
   shaders on first use ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ measure first-open vs steady-state frame cost
   per surface; pre-warm the worst (drunk overlay shader, distortion

5. Autosave/save stalls on web: coordinate with LA.1 item 5 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ this task
   owns measuring the user-visible hitch, LA.1 owns the fix.
```

## Epic C ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Dead Weight & Consistency

**LC.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Execute the Dead-Code & Dead-Asset Removal Sequence** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: L0.1 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text

TASK LC.1 - docs/plans/dead_code_audit_report.md prescribed a removal
sequence on 2026-07-01 and was explicitly read-only. Execute it against the

1. Re-verify first: the tree has moved since 2026-07-01 (0.3.1 landed 15
   tasks). For every item in the report's removal sequence, re-trace the
   references with the report's own method before deleting ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ an item that
```

**LC.2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Hot-Path GDScript Idiom & Typing Pass** ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ P2 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ deps: LA.1ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂ¦Гўв‚¬Е“LA.6 ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ status: BACKLOG

```text

TASK LC.2 - Measured micro-optimization of the hottest surviving functions.
This task runs LAST in Epic A/C order and only touches functions the sweeps
measured as still-hot; no blind style rewrites.

1. From the sweeps' disposition tables, take every function still costing
   >0.2ms/frame (dev box) or on the L0.2 red list. For each: static-type

   replace Variant Dictionary field access in inner loops with locals
```

## Epic D ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўв‚¬ЕЎГ‚В¬ГѓвЂљГ‚Вќ Gates & Close

```text
[PREPEND SHARED GUIDELINE]

TASK LD.2 - Close 0.3.2: full-gate rerun, evidence ledger, version stamp.

1. Rerun on the final tree: validate_project.ps1; check_godot.ps1
   -RequireGodot -Suite Full; every FoundationSuite; full perf probe with
   the LD.1 tightened budgets; foundation_soak_probe with LB.1's slope
   asserts (-SimMinutes 180); determinism probe (10 seeds); stuck sweep
   (200 seeds); 60-run mouse batch strict; all seed audits; the LD.1 web
   perf smoke; T73-TUNED12 endgame metrics reproduction.
2. Author docs/plans/0.3.2_release_checklist.md in the 0.3.1 style:
   before/after tables for every metric this board moved (per-surface
   draw, per-game resolve and surface_state, pinball feature tick + frame,
   music steady-state cost, soak slope, boot timeline desktop/web, web zip
   size, draw calls per surface), the function-census coverage summary
   (functions reviewed / fixed / waived per sweep), the removal ledger
   from LC.1, and accepted limitations (each with a named reason and
   owning future task).
3. Bump project.godot and export presets to 0.3.2; verify the version
   renders via the UI suite; export web and windows via export_itch.ps1
   and record artifact hashes and sizes (compare web zip to the 0.3.1
   16.3 MB / 0D26DE61ГѓЖ’Г†вЂ™ГѓвЂљГ‚ВўГѓЖ’Г‚ВўГѓВўГўвЂљВ¬Г…ВЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¬ГѓЖ’Гўв‚¬ЕЎГѓвЂљГ‚В¦ baseline).

DONE GATE: every command in step 1 green on the final tree; checklist
committed; exports packaged with hashes and sizes recorded.
```
